103.53a
drang srong rnam pa mang po la/ /tshogs 'di yon tan rgya cher bsgrags/ /don rnams nges par bshad pa las/ /drang srong mang pos rig 'dzin thob/ /ston par byed pa'i kal ya na/ /gsang bdag chos kyi rgyal por 'gyur/ /'on tang gsang ba'i don 'di dag / snod dang ldan pa'i 'gro ba la/ /bstan tam bshad dam brjod par gyis/ /des ni yon tan chen po dang / /nga yi spobs pa 'thob par 'gyur/ /des na 'dus pa chen po'i tshogs/ /rgyal ba kun gyi thugs dam ni/ /rnal 'byor gsang ba'i tshogs 'di yin/ /rnal 'byor gang zhig blo ldan pas/ /skad cig tsam 'am thang cig la/ /rgyal ba'i tshogs 'di rab bskrun na/ /rgyal ba sangs rgyas thams cad dang / /rig 'dzin rnal 'byor mtha' dag dang / /tha tshig zab mo skongs nas kyang / /chos kyi mig ni thob par 'gyur/ /des ni tshogs spyad yon tan dang / /log par spyad pa'i skyon rnams ni/ /sngon byung glengs gzhi bshad pa yin/ /zhes sems dpa'i rdo rjes gsungs so/ /rgyud kyi rgyal po rdo rje bkod pa kun 'dus rig pa'i mdo las 'das pa sngon byung gi le'u zhes bya ste bdun pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das sems dpa'i rdo rje de bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po de'i zhal du shin du re zhing bka' sdod pa'i tshul gyis lta zhing kun du brjid par 'khor gyis bskul ba'i sa la sta gon du gnas shing cang mi smra bar gyur to/ /de nas 'khor phal mo ches rnam par bskul bar rig nas rnal 'byor gyi phyag lus kun sa la brdabs nas a la la ho zhes bya ba'i sgra phyung nas mgrin gcig du gsol ba btab pa/ e ma rdo rje sems chen po/ /rang rig mkhyen pa'i ye shes 'bar/ /mgon po yon tan bsam las 'das/ /rgyal 'theb khyod la phyag 'tshal lo/ /e ma rang snang dbyer med sku/ /rnam dag bsod nams mtshan gyis brgyan/ /dpe byad 'bru bkod blta mi ngoms/ /sku lnga'i mchog la phyag 'tshal lo/ /e ma rnam dag
103.53b
nam mkha'i dbyings/ /gcig gsung sna tshogs sgrar rig mkhyen/ /bsam 'das brjod med rdo rje'i gsung / /gsung lnga'i mchog la phyag 'tshal lo/ /e ma gsang ba nam mkha'i thugs/ /mnyam nyid mi g.yo so sor gsal/ /kun rig snying po ye shes mchog /thugs lnga'i mchog la phyag 'tshal lo/ /e ma mi mdzad mdzad pa che/ /ma chags chags bral 'dod chags mdzod/ /thams cad sgrol ba'i las chen po/ /'phrin las mchog la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rgyal tshab khyod la gsol ba ni/ /byams mgon thugs rje'i byin brlabs kyis/ /sprul pa'i go tshags ru mnyam te/ /'khor ba'i skyas lings chen po la/ /sdug bsngal shin du gsad pa'i phyir/ /thams cad dur khrod chen po ru/ /byin gyis brlabs pa'i las chen mdzod/ /a ho zhes gsol ba btab pa las/ sems dpa' rdo rje chen po des rnal 'byor pa'i phyag byas nas/ bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po la zhus pa/ a la la ho bde ba chen po'i mchog gsang ba kun gyi rgyal po/ /yang gsang bla na med pa'i bdag nyid/ 'dus pa chen po'i tshogs rmad du byung ba'i tshig shin du rtul phod pa gsol pa 'tshal ba 'di shin du ngo mtshar lags so/ /'di dag 'dul ba'i dbang du dgongs te/ ji ltar 'tshal ba'i bsam pa rangs par mdzad du gsol zhes gsol ba btab pa las / bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po des kun du 'dul ba'i dus mkhyen nas bka' gsang rmad du byung ba'i 'khor gyis bskor ba dur khrod rgyan gyi rol pa las rmad du byung ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /snyoms par zhugs nas 'khor byin gyis rlob pa'i tshig 'di gsungs so/ /hU~M he he phaT/ hU~M hU~M bi shwa badzra kro d+ha dz+wa la maN Da la A ra li a li u li ta pa li tra~M s+t+wa~M/ kha li ho/ /na sha sta~M b+ha ya hU~M/ bru~M phu tsa khA hi phaT phaT ha la hU~M zhes gsungs so/ /'jig rten drug gi phyogs bcu
103.54a
mtha' yas pa thams cad dur khrod kyi dkyil 'khor du gyur nas/ g.yos/ rab tu g.yos/ shin du rnam par 'thor ro/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po des sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la 'khor gzhan gyis yid tshod du mi 'gyur ba'i sku'i chos bstan pa ni sku kun du dur khrod kyi bdag po chen por bsgyur nas dur khrod kyi gnas brgyad dang / he ru ka'i gnas bcu dang / dpal gyi chas brgyad dang / dur khrod kyi rgyan chen po dgu dang / don gyi rtag chen po bco brgyad dang / dur khrod kyi longs spyod sna tshogs pa bstan pas zhal 'dzum pa'i mdangs kyi gzigs pa las sems dpa' rdo rje des mkhyen te/ bka' gsang dbang chen 'dis don du ni bshad/ tshig du bsgrags par rig nas 'dus pa'i tshogs la shin tu ldem dgongs kyi tshig du smras pa/ bka' gsang rmad byung chen po 'di/ /sbas pas zab cing rtogs dka' ba/ /mtshon pas don 'byin mi shes pas/ /nyon mongs rang dga' spyod snyam pa'i/ /shin tu byis pa'i blo zhan pa'i/ /nges pa'i shes rab mig ldongs te/ /don gyi rtsal shugs chungs ba yis/ /dga' bde'i longs spyod bskrun snyam nas/ /mtshan ma rang dgar spyad bsgrubs kyang / /rang bzhin 'grub par mi 'gyur te/ /rgyud phung 'bras bu tshig gyur nas/ /myu gu brlag ste ga la 'byung / /gtan tshigs de bas 'di don dag /rtsal zhan dag la bstan min zhes/ /gsang bdag rgyal po kun gsung na/ /ci khyod rnams kyis mi shes sam/ /zhes rnam par smras pa las/ 'dus pa'i tshogs kyis slar gsol pa/ e ma 'o sems dpa' chen po de lta bu'i rgyu tshig chen po dag 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi nang dam pa 'dir gsung ngam/ 'on te mi spyod dam/ cang ma lags grang / ci blang dor mdzad dam/ e ma snod du ma gyur pa ni gang mchis/ thams cad byang chub kyi snying po can lags na/ thong kun du rab tu thong / rnam par rab tu gsungs/ 'gag pa mi mnga'
103.54b
mi 'gog gsungs/ /ci phyir mi gsung thogs med sras/ /rgyal ba'i sras po dus 'di lags/ /gsang ba'i snying po snong 'di lags/ /bka' gsang dkyil 'khor gnas 'di lags/ /gsang ba'i dur khrod tshul 'di lags/ /snying rje zher sems khyod la 'dud/ /gsang ba yang gsang khyod la 'dud/ /gsang ba ye gsang khyod la 'dud/ /dkyil 'khor rgyal po khyod la 'dud/ /'khor lo snying po khyod la 'dud/ /gsang chen snying po tshul ci lags/ /bka' gsang dkyil 'khor thabs ci lags/ /'bras bu bde ba'i don ci lags/ /ma 'ongs pa yi rnal 'byor dag /bsgrubs na dang len 'tshal ba yi/ /rig par 'gyur ba'i thabs ci lags/ /'byung chen rgyal pos bshad du gsol/ /zhes gsol ba btab pa las/ sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa de shin tu bzhad pa chen pos rnam par bzhad de/ a a he he'i gang rgyangs bsgrags pas 'khor thams cad kyang gad rgyangs kyi sgra chen po sgrogs par mdzad de/ dgyes pa'i 'od zer las shes rab kyi dpal de dgyes pa'i rol mo sna tshogs ling long phyad par byung ngo / /de nas sems dpa'i rdo rje dam pa des lus kun bsrang ste/ dur khrod kyi chas sna tshogs bsar zhing rtags bcwa brgyad 'bar bar byas nas brjid pa'i gsung gis gsang sngags rgya mtsho dang / rnam grangs sna tshogs don gyi bsgrub pa rtags kyi rol pa gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po 'di dag bshad do/ /gcig du yang dag nges grub pa'i/ /don la rton byed rnal 'byor rnams/ /thogs med nyid du 'grub 'dod pa/ /ji ltar btso blag mkhan dag gis/ /ras dkar sbyangs pas tshon 'jen ltar/ /rnal 'byor las rnams dang por ni/ /skongs dang sbyong ba'i las rnams gces/ /zab mor 'jug pa'i sngon logs nas/ /sems nyid gting nas tshar gcad phyir/ /theg pa dman pa'i skye bo dang / /lhan cig ci la 'ang mi brnal lo/ /de las gyur pa'i yo byad dag /rus sbal mgo la 'ongs pa dag /shin tu 'khrugs pa'i sems chen gyis/ /rgya mtshos bshugs te spang bar bya/ /gal te
103.55a
gang zag dbang gis ni/ /nyams pa'i chad pa byung ba na/ /mgon tshun chos nyid chu phab nas/ /skong zlog cho ga rgya cher bya/ /sgrub rtsom sngon nam yang sngon nam/ /zhag grangs dag gi sngon logs nas/ /sdigs sbyangs byang chub sems bskyed de/ /dge ba'i don la 'dun par bya/ /slong mo dang slong la dga' ba/ /slong la 'tsho ba'i tshe spyod rnams/ /sde dang tshan dang grar byas te/ /snying rje khud pa'i zhing du bya/ /sman dang 'bru dang rtsi rnams dang / /bcud kyi mchog du gyur pa dag /btags sam phye mar sbyar nas kyang / /klung ngam chu klung mtsho chen du/ /dor te chags med sbyin par bya/ /dge ba'i yon bdag dang blangs te/ /nad gso shes slob spyod sgom grwa/ /btsugs te bsti gnas mchog bya zhing / /dus kyi 'khor lo'i mchod chen bya/ /gsung sgra rgya mtsho sgrogs pa yis/ /glegs bam zab mo kun bsten te/ /brjod dang bsnyen bkur bsti gnas kyis/ /rgya che yangs pa'i las rnams bya/ /ye shes tshogs rnams rdzogs bya'i phyir/ /shes rab tshogs kyi sbyin mchog dag / bstan tam glegs bam la sogs pa'i/ /blo mchog ldan pa rnams la sbyin/ /bsgom dang goms par bya ba yin/ /kun gzhi dag par bya ba'i phyir/ /ting 'dzin bye ba mang po la/ /blo mchog yid kyi rtsal de sbyang / /chos kyi 'khor lo rab bskor to/ /rgyud sbyang lhag pa'i shes rab blta/ /sho gam srang dang sho gam lam/ /mi bde'i gnod pa kun bsal te/ /tshad med snying rje'i 'khor lo bskor/ /sbyin pa'i 'khor lo rgyun mi gcad/ /chu'am sa 'am nam mkha' 'am/ /me 'am de bzhin rlung rnams la/ /sku gdung spel mchod ring bsrel rnams/ /brtsam pa'i las chen 'khor lor bya/ /mtshams med zlogs par byed pa yi/ /lus sems rgyud la rdul rlags te/ /'phags pa'i sbrin tshogs pho brang du/ /rdul snyed lus kyis mchod sems bshags/ /rgyal mnyes las ni gyis shig pa/ /thabs chen spyod pa'i las chen las/ /rnam bzhi me yi las mchog bya/ /
103.55b
des ni mtshams med zlogs pa yin/ /thugs rje 'byung ba'i 'khor lo dag /gang ltar goms ltar 'bad rtsol bya/ /bstan pa skyong ba'i tshogs rnams la/ /sbyin mchod spel ba'i las rnams bya/ /de la sogs pa'i dge ba'i tshogs/ /don du mi 'gyur kun spangs la/ /nan tan tshogs kyi dpung chen bskyed/ /'di ltar las chen ltang sogs pa/ /gzhan du bskyed pa ma yin te/ /rtse gcig don ldan rnal 'byor pa/ /rgyud ldan snod ldan bya phyir dang / /gal te rtsal zhan ma grub na/ /dge bsags ltang chen kun bsdoms te/ /las kyi bsags pa don bgrangs shing / /gdung ba'i shugs phyung rtsal sprugs nas/ /nyi shar chu klung zla brnyan ltar/ /rang bzhin shugs kyis 'grub par gces/ /de phyir phra mo yan chad kyang / /bdag gi don du 'gyur bar bya/ /de ltar spyad pa spyod pa yi/ /phra mo'i rnal 'byor blo 'phel ba/ /chung ngu chung sogs mthar zad nas/ /skong ba'i rnal 'byor 'khor lo yis/ /zhig dang ral dang chag 'dres dag /bkang gso gzhug pa'i las 'di bya/ /las chen skong ba'i khyad par gyis/ /gnas su brtag par nges med de/ /mi sdug skyon can bkra mi shis/ /spangs te med par gyur ba yi/ /shin du sar pa'i gnas chen dag /bkang ba'i gnas su de 'gyur ro/ /de ltar yid 'ong gnas btsal nas/ /drod ldan bla ma spyan drangs te/ /sri zhu rgyal chos spyi bor bkur/ /de yang dmigs kyis zhu ba dag /maN Dal khar gsil tsam dag la/ /me long snying po ltar byas te/ /gtsang ma'i rgyu las rdzas byas pa/ /yid 'ong rnam lnga'i mchod pa la/ /rkyen gyi rnal 'byor sna tshogs kyis/ /brgyan te klubs pa'i sprin phung rnams/ /mnyes nas skongs phyir rgyal la dbul/ /phyi 'khor skyong ba'i mgon po la/ /'dod yon lnga la sogs pa yi/ /yid bzhin longs spyod rkyen dang bcas/ /yon tan cha las smon bcol mchod/ /mnyes nas skongs ba'i stongs su 'gyur/ khams gsum snying rje'i gnas rnams la/ /yo byad sbyin tshogs
103.56a
chen po las/ /'dod pa'i bsam pa rangs byas na/ /mgu bas skongs pa'i stongs su 'gyur/ /bgegs su gyur pa'i bgegs ris kyang / /mnyam pa'i don gyis sems mi dbyung / /dmigs kyis kha zas sna tshogs las/ /bgegs rnams mgu na thams cad kyang / /mnyam pa'i don gyis skongs pa'i rgyur/ /cung zad tsam du snang ba yin/ /de ltar skongs ba'i las rnams kyis/ /bskang bar bya ba'i dmigs rnams ni/ /rnam pa ldar ni snang ba ste/ /kun tu nyams pa chen po dang / /rtsa ba nyams dang yan lag nyams/ /de bzhin zlas nyams zhar nyams lnga/ /bskang ba'i thabs kyang lnga yod de/ /spyad pa'i las kyis bskang ba dang / /rdzas dang don dang ting 'dzin dang / /man ngag gsang ba'i thabs chen no/ /de dag la yang lnga lnga ste/ /spyod pa'i tshul gyis bskang ba la/ /rnam pa lnga ru bshad par bya/ /dang po 'bum lnga khri gsum ste/ /rtsa nyams khri lnga stong gsum mo/ /yan lag nyams par gyur pa la/ /stong lnga brgya gsum thon par bya/ /zlas nyams lnga brgya bcu gsum mo/ /zhar gyis nyams par gyur pa la/ /bcu lnga gcig gsum dag gis skongs/ /rdzas kyis bskang ba'i thabs mchog ni/ /gal te bsrung ba 'ga' zhig las/ /byang chub tha tshig ral gyur na/ /gti mug rigs kyi tha tshig bkang / /dmangs rigs bla ma spyan drangs la/ /nyes 'gal mi bcab stong du bshags/ /gser la sogs pa'i rdzas chen gyis/ /tha tshig gang brlag nor des blu/ /byang chub sems bskyed rgyud sbyang mnyan/ /rdo rje tha tshig ral gyur na/ /zhe sdang rigs kyi tha tshig bkang / /rje'u rigs bla ma spyan drangs te/ /nyes byas mi bcab 'bum du bshags/ /shel la sogs pa'i rdzas chen gyis/ /tha tshig gang brlag nor des blu/ /bsam gtan ting 'dzin bsgom brtson bya/ /rin chen tha tshig nyams gyur na/ /nga rgyal rigs kyi tha tshig bkang / /rgyal rigs bla ma spyan drangs te/ /nyes byas mi bcab brgyad khrir bshags/ /
103.56b
bai dUr la sogs rdzas chen gyis/ /tha tshigs gang brlag nor des blu/ /sku gdung ring bsrel rnam par spel/ /pad ma'i tha tshig rol gyur na/ /'dod chags rigs kyi tha tshig bkang / /gdol rigs bla ma spyan drangs la/ /nyes byas mi bcab brgyar bshags bya/ /byi ru la sogs rdzas chen gyis/ /tha tshig gang brlag nor des slu/ /bshad bya zab mo'i glegs bam brjod/ /las kyi tha tshig ral gyur na/ /phrag dog rigs kyi tha tshigs bskang / /bram ze rigs bshes spyan drangs la/ /nyes byas mi bcab bcu lngar bshags/ /in dra la sogs rdzas rnams kyis/ /tha tshig gang brlag nor des blu/ /mchod sbyin bsod nams las chen bya/ /des ni bskang ba'i las chen 'grub/ /don gyis bskang ba'i thabs mchog kyang / /rnam lnga'i tshul du bshad par bya/ /chos kun nam mkhar bsgom nas kyang / /bag chags bzang ngan thams cad kun/ /ci yang med par blo la gzhag /de la goms byas nyes pa med/ /kun la mkhas pa'i bla ma la/ /rgya che yangs pa'i chos mnyan te/ /bsam pa'i las rnams rgya cher bya/ /yid kyis dmigs pa'i las dag na/ /rtsa ba nyams pa skongs bar 'gyur/ /gal te yan lag nyams gyur na/ /chos nyid nam mkha'i don ston pa'i/ /glegs bam zab mo kun brtags te/ /don rnams rgya cher brtag par bya/ /des ni yan lag nyams pa med/ /zlas na tha tshig nyams 'gyur na/ /bla ma skyes bu mkhas pa la/ /gzhung chen tshugs pa'i bstan pa zhig /ston pa'i yon bdag gnyer blangs te/ /blo yi rtsal can kun bsdus te/ /dam chos bdud rtsi bstan pa bsgrags/ /gal te zhar gyis nyams gyur na/ /bstan pa'i glegs bam rgya chen rnams/ /bris nas chos kyi sbyin par bya/ /des ni zhar nyams skongs par 'gyur/ /ting 'dzin rtsal gyi thabs mchog ni/ /bag chags can gyi spyi gtsug du/ /rtsa dmar 'od ni me long tsam/ /
103.57a

103.57b

103.60b

103.61b
ldan dam tshig 'gal 'gyur te/ /dang po'i tha tshig bka' la btags pa'i tshe/ /bka' la ma gus 'gal bgyis dpyas long btogs/ /bar du bslab pa'i gnyer chen phog pa'i tshe/ /bslab la mi brtson don la g.yel ba dang / /tha ma 'di tshe 'bras bu sgrub pa na/ /bka' dang gzhung bzhin ma lcogs don las 'gal/ /tshor dang ma tshor sgrib pa che chung rnams/ /shin tu mi shes ma rigs dbang gis na/ /ston pa'i bka' dang dam las 'gal bgyis pa/ /dpa' bo thugs rje'i bdag la bzod par gsol/ /'khor ba thog ma med pa'i dus mtha' nas/ /las kyi dbang gis bdag cag ring du 'khyams/ /nyon mongs log par lta ba'i dug 'thungs te/ /sdug bsngal nad kyis shin tu gdungs pa la/ /bde gshegs thugs rje sman pa'i rgyal po yis/ /dam tshig bdud rtsi thar pa'i sman stsal bas/ /nyon mongs 'khrul pa'i nad rnams zhi mdzad cing / /bla med byang chub snying por 'tsho mdzad pa/ /byams mgon thugs rje'i bdag la skyabs su mchi zhes ngus nas/ a la la ho zhes brjod de gnyen po drag por bsten nas lus gdan khrir phul te/ byang chub sems kyis rnam par 'dud pa'i don la rnam par sbyangs pas lus gcer bu zang mar phyung / gnong ba drag po'i 'gyod pa byas pas bde bar gshegs pa rnams mnyes par gyur to/ /des sgrib pa byang zhing bsod nams kyi tshogs rdzogs pa'i rtags lus gos dang phral nas ldan pa'i thod pa yang zla ba tshes brgyad par gyur to/ /sa thob pa'i rtags su de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhabs rten du gnas par gyur to/ /de nas sems dpa'i rdo rje dgyes te bka' stsal pa/ mi'i thod pa can rnams 'gyod pa'i las kyis bshags pa legs te/ nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag par gyur to/ /da ni shes bya'i sgrib pa dag cing ye shes kyi tshogs rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir nyan pa'i dbang pos sangs rgyas kyis gsung la gsang sngags kyi sgra rnams nyon cig /des ni sa nas sar 'phar zhing 'bras bu yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro/ /de skad ces gsungs pas 'khor bsam pa
103.62a
rangs par gyur to/ /rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po rdo rje bkod pa kun 'dus rig pa'i mdo las skong ba las kyi bsgrub lugs kyi le'u ste brgyad pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog nyid ting nge 'dzin rgyas shing rnam par 'phrul ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po yang ting nge 'dzin rnam par 'phrul pa zhes bya ba la snyoms par zhugs so/ /'dus pa'i 'khor rnams kyang sna tshogs 'phrul pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /de nas 'dus pa phal mo che'i 'khor gyis chos thams cad ci yang med par mthong ngo / /chos thams cad ci yang med par gsal bar gyur pa dang / chos nyid stong pa'i nam mkha' las brag ca'i tshul du sgra 'di byung ngo / /mi gnas mi rtog bsam dang bral/ /ma chags chags bral yul las 'das/ /ci yang mi 'byung cir ma yin/ /rang byung rang zhi brjod dang bral/ /zhes sgra byung bas ston pa ni don gyi che ba phyung / 'khor rnams ni rtsal sbyangs/ thams cad don la ngam zhing chos nyid kyi nam mkha' mthong ngo / /de nas bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po nyid snying rje rgyun gyi ting nge 'dzin zhes bya ba la snyoms par zhugs so/ /de nas chos nyid kyi nam mkha' la snying rje byang chub sems kyi gzugs brnyan nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor zhig shar bar gyur to/ /de nas 'dus pa phal mo che'i 'khor rnams yang dag par rtog pa 'di ltar skyes te/ e ma chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin 'di ltar yin pa las 'di ltar ma shes pa'i 'gro ba rnams 'khor ba'i rgya mtshor bying ba 'di yang snying rje zhes snying rje byang chub kyi sems skyes par gyur to/ /de nas nyi ma'i snying po'i 'od zer las cho 'phrul gyi sgra phyung ngo / /yongs la khyab pa'i nyi ma'i 'od/ /snying rje byang chub sems yin te/ /rnam rtog mun pa sel bar snang / /yid bzhin rin chen 'bar ba'o zhes sgra byung ba las chos thams cad byang chub sems kyi 'od zer du gsal bar gyur to/ /de nas yang bcom ldan 'das gsang ba'i mchog gi bdag po de nyid cho 'phrul 'byung ba'i rgyu zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms
103.62b
par zhugs so/ /de nas 'dus pa phal mo che'i 'khor rnams kyis nyi ma'i snying po las chos thams cad kyi rgyu yi ge a dkar po shar bar mthong ngo / /de nas a la cho 'phrul sgra byung ngo / /a'i chags med yi ge'i mdzod/ /cho 'phrul rtog pa kun gyi rgyu/ /nyon mongs skyon bral zla ba'i mdog /cho 'phrul sna tshogs 'byung ba'i rgyu/ /zhes sgra byung bas 'dus pa'i tshogs rnams kyis chos thams cad cho 'phrul gyi rang bzhin du gnas par mthong ngo / /de nas bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po de ci yang mi mdzad pa cho 'phrul sna tshogs kyi rang bzhin du snang bar gyur to/ /de nas yum chen mo nam mkha'i dbyings phyug ma zhes bya ba de chos thams cad nam mkha'i b+ha gar byin gyis brlob pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /zhugs par gyur pa dang 'dus pa phal mo che'i 'khor gyis chos thams cad nam mkha' khyab pa'i rang bzhin du mthong ngo / /de nas yum gyi b+ha ga'i snying po las 'od zer mthing ka 'phros nas nyi ma'i snying po'i a la bskul bas yi ge e mthing ka 'phros te lding zhing gnas pa las cho 'phrul gyi rang sgra 'di byung ngo / /a ni e yi rang bzhin te/ /a las e byung mkha' khyab bdal/ /mi 'gyur thogs med bsam las 'das/ /mtha' dang dbus med kun tu bdal/ /zhes sgra byung bas/ thams cad nam mkha'i rang bzhin du phyam chad par gyur to/ /de nas yang yum chen mo las kyi dbyings phyug mas yang zhing g.yo ba rlung gi dkyil 'khor zhes bya ba la snyoms par zhugs so/ /des 'dus pa phal mo che'i 'khor gyis chos thams cad rlung gi rang bzhin du gnas par mthong ngo / /de nas rlung de las cho 'phrul gyi sgra byung ngo / /a yi byin brlabs ye shes las/ /rlung gi cho 'phrul ya~M du shar/ /thams cad 'degs pa'i stobs ldan zhing / /rang bzhin g.yo zhing thogs med 'phyo/ /zhes sgra byung bas rlung gi dkyil 'khor du 'khyil bar gyur to/ /de nas yum chos kyi dbyings phyug ma zhes bya des 'bar 'phro
103.63a
me'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /'dus pa phal mo che'i 'khor gyis chos thams cad me'i rang bzhin du gnas par mthong ngo / /de nas me'i 'od zer la cho 'phrul gyi sgra byung ba/ a yi byin brlabs ye shes las/ /cho 'phrul me yi snying por shar/ /'bar bas gsal byed ye shes 'phro/ /dngos po kun zang me klong 'tshub/ /ces sgra byung bas me'i bskal pa 'byam klas so/ /de nas yang yum rin chen dbyings phyug ma zhes bya ba des sdud pa rgya mtsho'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /des 'dus pa phal mo che'i 'khor gyi chos thams cad chu'i rang bzhin du gnas par mthong ngo / /de nas rlabs kyi 'od zer las cho 'phrul gyi sgra 'di byung ngo / /rgyu yi yi ge 'od zer las/ /chu yi snying po'i cho 'phrul shar/ /nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'o/ /rlung mtsho thams cad rgyas par 'gyur/ /zhes sgra byung bas thams cad yum rin chen dbyings phyug ma'i rang bzhin gyis khyab par gnas so/ /de nas yum chen mo rdo rje dbyings phyug ma zhes bya bas zhing khams thams cad byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /de nas 'dus pa phal mo che'i 'khor gyis chos thams cad sa rnams yongs su rdzogs pa'i rang bzhin du mthong ngo / /de nas sa rdo rje 'bar ba zhes bya ba las cho 'phrul gyi sgra byung ba/ mi dmigs pa la sna tshogs par/ /snang ba'i cho 'phrul 'di byung ba/ /rnal 'byor sa bcu rdzogs pa'i don/ /lhun gyis grub pas bde ba che/ /zhes sgra byung bas sa dgu 'dul ba'i bye brag tu thugs su chud par gyur to/ /de nas sems dpa'i rdo rje snying po de ri bo brtsegs pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /des 'dus pa phal mo che'i 'khor gyis chos thams cad rdo rje 'bar ba'i ri bor mthong ngo / /de nas de'i 'od las cho 'phrul gyi sgra 'di byung ngo / /rnam dag shes rab mkha' klong nas/ /rdo rje 'bar ba'i ri bo shar/ /rgya che gting zab nam 'phang gcod/ /rtog pa'i ri bo 'joms par byed ces sgra byung bas
103.63b
rdo rje 'bar ba'i ri bos nyon mongs pa'i ri bo thams cad zil gyis mnan no/ /de nas dbyings phyug ma chen mo lnga/ /shes rab zab mo'i gzhal yas yum gyi mkha' klong rnam dag ces bya pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /b+ha ga'i snying po las cho 'phrul gyi sgra 'di byung ngo / /b+ha ga gsang ba'i 'od zer las/ /bde gshegs bzhugs pa'i gzhal yas khang / /nam mkha'i mtha' ltar dpag tu med/ /dus gsum rgyal ba'i rgya mtsho'i dbyings zhes sgra byung ngo / /byung bas nam mkha' thams cad pho brang gi gzhal yas 'byam klas par gyur to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog de nyid chos thams cad sku la yongs su rdzogs pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin nam phyag rgya thams cad rnam par spro ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /de nas 'dus pa phal mo che'i 'khor rnams kyis 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i chos thams cad bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po'i zhabs kyi gdan khri yan chad nas dbu'i gtsug tor man chad du rdzogs par mthong ngo / /de nas yang 'khor ba 'dod pa khams ni chags pa khrag gi rgya mtshor rdzogs/ 'khor ba gzugs kyi khams ni zhing chen gyi sa gzhi bdal ba la rdzogs par mthong ngo / /keng rus la gzugs med pa'i khams rdzogs par mthong ngo / /ri rab kyi kha mu tig gi bcal dang / asma gar ba'i 'bar ba'i 'od 'khrigs pa'i nor bu rin po che 'bar ba'i brag gtams pa la/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams rdzogs par mthong ngo / /nor bu rin po che'i steng na rdo rje rtse gsum dang rtse lnga'i brag gtams pa la kri ya dang u pa ya dang yo ga rnams rdzogs par mthong ngo / /rdo rje brag chen gyi steng na pad ma dkar po'i maN Dal la bskyed pa'i rnal 'byor pa thams cad rdzogs par mthong ngo / /pad ma'i steng na nyi ma nyi shu rtsa bzhi dang / zla ba nyi shu rtsa bzhi kha sbyor du bkod pa la dbang phyug pho nyi shu rtsa bzhi dang / mo nyi shu rtsa bzhi rdzogs par mthong ngo / /dbang phyug pho mo'i steng byol song gi gtso bo brgyad ni rig 'dzin chen
103.64a
po'i rnal 'byor nyon mongs pa sbyangs nas shes bya'i sgrib pa sbyang ba'i phyir dpa' brtun stag dang / 'jigs byed seng ge dang / gdug pa'i gzig dang / gtum po'i dom dang / stobs kyi glang po dang / brjid pa'i ma he dang / 'dzin pa'i chu srin dang / zhe sdang gi sbrul rnams la rig 'dzin thams cad sa la yongs su rdzogs par mthong ngo/ /gzhal yas chen po 'bar ba la yum kun du bzang mo rdzogs par mthong ngo/ /me dpung chen po dgu la ye shes kyi sgo dgu rtseg gu yongs su 'bar bar rdzogs par mthong ngo/ /zhabs brgyad la gsang ba'i yum bzhi dang / sgo ma bzhi rdzogs par mthong ngo/ /dur khrod kyi rgyan chen po bcwa brgyad ni ma mo chen mo bcwa brgyad yongs su rdzogs par gsal lo/ /phyag mtshan bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis ni 'phra men ma bcu dbyug pa 'phyar ba'i lag na khyung bcu 'bar ba'i kha nas mtshon cha sna tshogs 'phro ba/ mkha' 'gro brgyad dbyug pa 'phyar ba'i lag na seng ge kha glal ba brgyad kyi kha nas ral gri 'bar ba brgyad 'phro ba/ shugs 'gro brgyad dbyug par 'phyar ba'i lag na stag mche ba gtsigs pa brgyad kyi kha nas rdo rje sna tshogs 'phro ba/ ma mo brgyad dbyug par 'phyar ba'i lag na mi mgo brgyad rdo rje lu gu rgyud kyis btags nas klad la bskor ba/ 'bar ma brgyad dbyug pa 'phyar ba'i lag na me dpung 'bar ba brgyad las thu lum 'phro ba ste/ bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis su gsal lo/ /phyag bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis ni khrag 'thung 'bar ba bzhi/ ging pho dgu/ mo dgu/ za byed pha bcu gsod byed ma bcu ste bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis su gsal lo/ /zhal nyi shu rtsa gcig ni srid pa za byed gsang ba'i dur khrod nyi shu rtsa gcig tu gsal lo/ /spyan 'bar ba drug bcu rtsa bzhi ni he ru ka yab yum drug bcu rtsa bzhir gsal lo/ /dbu nyi shu rtsa gcig ni dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas nyi shu rtsa gcig du gsal lo/ /g.yas kyi dbu bdun gyi spyi gtsug nas sangs rgyas kyi sku re re byung ba'i dbu la 'khor lo 'od zer dang bcas pa re re
103.64b
'bar ba/ dbus kyi dbu bdun las dbu rgyan sangs rgyas kyi dbu re re byung ba'i sku la rin po che'i mchod rten 'bar ba bdun du gsal ba/ g.yon gyi dbu bdun las dbu rgyan sangs rgyas kyi sku re re byung ba'i dbu la nor bu rin po che bdun du gsal ba/ 'khor lo dang mchod rten dang / rin po che de dag gi lte ba dang / bum pa dang / rtse mo las rgyal mtshan chen po bcu 'bar ba ni rgya bye'u lcags kyi rgyal mtshan dang / gdul bya sha ba'i rgyal mtshan dang / gcan zan gzig gi rgyal mtshan dang / sprul pa rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan dang / rin chen sbrul nag gi rgyal mtshan dang / dpa' bo stag gi rgyal mtshan dang / gzi mdangs mi'i rgyal mtshan dang / dmar gsal khrag gi rgyal mtshan dang rtsal chen seng ge'i rgyal mtshan dang / gtum chen dom gyi rgyal mtshan dang / rgyal mtshan de rnams kyi rtse mo gcig tu 'dus te/ gser gyi gtsug tor tog stong 'bar ba'o/ /de nas 'dus pa phal mo che'i 'khor gyis zhabs kyi gdan khri yan chad nas dbu'i gtsug tor man chad du yongs su rdzogs par mthong ngo / /dbu las byung ba'i sangs rgyas nyi shu rtsa gcig dang / rgyal mtshan chen po bcu la rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor yongs su rdzogs par mthong ngo / /dbu'i gtsug tor rgyal mtshan gyi rtse mo la gser gyi tog stong ni rdzogs pa chen po'i rnal 'byor nyid du gsal bar mthong ngo / /de ltar mthong zhing gsal bar gyur pa dang / chos thams cad sku la yongs su rdzogs pa'i don la 'khor thams cad ngam zhing ngo mtshar skyes par gyur to/ /rnal 'byor chen po rnams kyi sku la yongs su bstod pa/ e ma'o chos kun sku la yongs su rdzogs pas chos kyi sku/ /rdo rje che mchog phyag 'tshal he ru ka /chos nyid mkha' la skar tshogs rgyas pa'i sku/ /dbyar gyi char sprin gtibs pa lta bu'i gzugs/ /chu rlabs lta bur brjod pa'i zhal gdangs shing / /nyi ma 'bum gyi 'od zer bdal ba bzhin/ /theg chen dgu dang 'khor ba'i chos rnams kun/ /phyag rgya gcig tu bkod nas rdzogs pa'i sku/ /sku gsum lhun grub chos sku tog
103.65a
stong 'bar/ /dbu skra kham nag ral pa'i gcod pan can/ /klu rgyal 'bum gyis klubs shing mchod kun 'bul/ /rdo rje gsung gis ljags sgra brdabs pas kyang / /hU~M dang phaT kyi sgra skad 'jigs par sgrogs/ /theg chen don dam gsang sngags sgrogs pa'i tshig /'bar ba'i smig ma mun rum glog ltar 'gyu/ /spyan dmar bzlog pa'i sdang mig nyi ltar 'bar/ /'bar ba'i shangs nas bskal pa'i tshub nag 'khyil/ /rdo rje thog dang gnam lcags ser chen 'bebs/ /rno dbal ma che ba zang yag gtsigs pa yis/ /nyon mongs log lta'i tshogs la ngam zhing 'khrug /thod rus sha khrag rkang rus 'bu dang rnag /za byed rngam pa'i zhal du chem chem gsol/ /sbrul gdug ko rlon la sogs 'jigs pa'i rgyan/ /rngam pa'i sku la shin tu brjid par brgyan/ /za byed rngam dang 'jigs byed mang po'i tshogs/ /'bar ba'i phyag mtshan sprul pa'i pho nya mdzad/ /'khor ba kun dang thar pa'i chos rnams kun/ /dpa' bo chen po'i gdan du brjid cing rol/ /'gran gyi zla med che btsan gcig pu nyid/ /gsang mchog 'bar ba'i sku la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /de skad ces bstod pas chos thams cad sku la yongs su rdzogs shing sangs ma rgyas pa med par gyur to/ /de nas yang bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po de nyid phyag rgya thams cad phyag rgya bkod pa'i pho brang du gyur to/ /spro ba rgyun gyi ting nge 'dzin zhes bya'o/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das gsang ba'i mchog bdag po chos nyid rgyun gyi ting nge 'dzin zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /chos kyi rgyun gyi ting nge 'dzin 'di gsungs so/ /nam mkha' don gyi glegs bam la/ /skar tshogs rig pa'i yig bris te/ /'byung chen bzhi'i sgra bsgrags pas/ /gsang sngags chos kyi rgyun mi 'chad/ /chos kyi rgyun gyi ting nge 'dzin zhes bya ba yongs su rdzogs so/ /de nas yang bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po des bdud rtsi rgyun gyi ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te 'di skad ces gsungs so/ /

103.66a
bcas/ /'di yang chos sku rgyun mi chad/ /sems dpa'i rdo rje des yang 'di skad ces gsungs so/ /'dzugs pa'i yan lag bzhi rmang rten/ /'khor lo tshogs chen khri 'phang brtan/ /yan lag dang po bum rten bcas/ /lcang lo gcod pan phreng bas klubs zhes gsungs so/ /de nas sems dpa'i rdo rje snying po des shi ba yongs su slong ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /ro yi sgrub lugs chen po ni/ /dur khrod chen po'i gnas rnams su/ /ro yi rdzas rnams btsal nas kyang / /'dod pa bsgyur ba'i sngags kyis gdab/ /ro yis steng du gnas nas ni/ /ro yi gnyen bor bdag bsams nas/ /ro sngags rgyun mi 'chad par bzlas/ /ro la bkrag dang mdangs byung na/ /grub par 'gyur ba'i rtags yin te/ /rgyun mi 'chad par ting 'dzin bya/ /ro ni 'gul bar gyur pa dang / /gser 'gyur rtsis ni byug par bya/ /ro yi yan lag kun bcings nas/ /sngags ni dag par bzlas par bya/ /ro nyid langs par gyur pa dang / /ro yi cho 'phrul ston par byed/ /brtul zhugs ldan pa'i skyes bu yis/ /de tshe ro yi lce bcad nas/ /ro la brdabs na gser du 'gyur/ /de bzhin ji ltar 'dod pa yi/ /rkyen gyis bsgyur na de ltar 'gyur/ /lce bcad ral gri mtshon cha des/ /ro yis ban da bcad pa dang / /ji ltar 'dod pa'i rdzas 'grub ste/ /ban da go ru bzur nas ni/ /lce yi ral gri thogs nas ni/ /lha min g.yul yang bzlog par 'gyur/ /ro langs grub pa'i rkang mgyogs ni/ /dpag pa'i tshad las 'das pa ste/ /skyes bu rtsal dang ldan pa bzhis/ /phyogs bzhi dag tu kha bltas nas/ /dus gcig mda' yi rgyang 'phangs nas/ /mda' ni sa la ma babs par/ /bzhi ka bar snang las blangs nas/ /skad cig tsam gyis 'jig rten skor/ /skyes bu lag tshod ma yal bar/ /de ma thag tu gnas su slebs/ /ro la 'dod pa kun 'byung zhes/ /dus gsum rgyal ba rnams kyis bshad ces gsungs so/ /ro langs bsgrub pa'i ting nge 'dzin to/ /de nas yang sems
103.66b
dpa'i rdo rje snying po de rdo rje nam mkha'i them skas zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas 'di skad ces gsungs so/ /nam mkha' rdo rjer bsgoms nas kyang / /ting 'dzin red bar gyur pa na/ /phan phun gya gyu'i thabs tshul du/ /rdo rje skas la bgrod nas ni/ /nam mkha'i dbyings su song nas kyang / /snang srid 'jig rten khams la blta/ /des ni sems yul yangs par 'gyur zhes gsungs so/ /de nas yang sems dpa'i rdo rje snying po de rgya mtsho chen po gnon pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te 'di skad ces gsungs so/ /rgya mtsho rdo rjes gtams par ni/ /ting 'dzin gsal bar gyur pa dang / /rgya mtsho chen por bgrod na ni/ /rgya mtshor gnas pa'i sems can rnams/ /ting 'dzin rdo rjes bsgral bar bya zhes gsungs so/ /de nas yang sems dpa'i rdo rje snying po de thogs med rlung zla'i dkyil 'khor la snyoms par zhugs nas 'di skad ces gsungs so/ /nam mkha' dag gi ling ga la/ /zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par/ /bsgom te ting 'dzin rtas pa dang / /zhing khams kun du bgrod par bya zhes gsungs so/ /de nas yang sems dpa'i rdo rje snying po des nyi ma rab tu snang ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas 'di skad ces gsungs so/ /nam mkha' dag gi ling ga la/ /nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par/ /bsgoms te ting 'dzin rtas pa dang / /mun pa'i gnas rnams thams cad bsal zhes gsungs so/ /de nas yang sems dpa'i rdo rje snying po des sreg pa'i bskal pa gzhil ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /rnal 'byor sdig 'dzub rtse mo la/ /zla ba'i dkyil 'khor 'od gsal 'bar/ /bsgoms te ting 'dzin rtas pa dang / /chu rgyun babs te gzhil bar bya zhes gsungs so/ /de nas yang sems dpa'i rdo rje snying po des stong gi 'jig rten rgyang mar 'phen pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te 'di skad ces gsungs so/ /rnal 'byor las kyi dkyil 'khor du/ /stong gi 'jig rten 'khor yug bcas/ /shin tu gsal bar bsgoms pa dang / /
103.67a

103.67b

103.71a
kyang / /bcwa lnga 'am yang na bdun bar du/ /tho rangs thun tha'i dang po'i tshe/ /rig 'dzin rnal 'byor sgrub pa po/ /shar gyi phyogs su kha bltas te/ /shar phyogs nam mkhas bsdus pa yi/ /lha klu gnod sbyin 'jig rten bcas/ /thams cad khong du bsdus nas kyang / /dbugs de slar la mi dbyung bar/ /rang gi khong du bstim par bya/ /tha mar sna yi nang du bsre/ /de ltar mang por bsgrubs pa dang / /dpal che gzi brjid thams cad 'thob/ /ces gsungs so/ /de nas yang sems dpa'i rdo rje snying po des rten pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas 'di skad ces gsungs so/ /gang zhig rten la gnas 'dod pa/ /mtshan ma bzang po'i gnas mchog tu/ /thams cad 'byor bar byas nas ni/ /sa las byas pa'i stegs bu bshams/ /dbus kyi pad ma 'dab brgyad la/ /zla gam dmar po sgo bzhir ldan/ /mtha' ma rdo rje ra bas bskor/ /dpal ldan tshe yi phyag rgya dgod/ /rin chen lugs kyi bum pa la/ /tshe rdzas rgyas par byas nas ni/ /mtshan ldan snod kyis kha dgab bya/ /rdo rje gzungs kyis btags nas ni/ /tshe tshad med par mnga' gsol la/ /dbus su de bzhin bzhag par bya/ /rin chen bum pa bzhi rnams la/ /gsang ba'i bu mo bzhi bkod gzhag /ya mtshan byung ba'i bum pa la/ /rigs bzhi sangs rgyas yab yum dang / /so so'i 'khor gyi sems dpa' rnams/ /thabs dang shes rab sdebs nas ni/ /phyogs phyogs gnas su tshom bur bri/ /sgo bzhir sgo ma bzhi rnams gzhag /sems kyi phyag rgya kun bkod nas/ /nyi zla ga 'ur a yu ni/ /'khyil 'bar 'tsher zhing gsal bar bya/ /a yu byang chub sems su zhu/ /rgyal mtshan mchog ldan rin chen gter/ /dbang bskur dpal ldan mdzod ldan ma/ /gsang ba'i bu mo tshe gter 'dzin/ /a yu yum bzhi'i thugs kang 'phros/ /de bzhin tshom bu rim par brgyud/ /rdo rje tshe mchog kun bsdus nas/ /

103.75b

bya'o/ /bud med chags pa'i rang bzhin te/ /chags pa khrag gi rgya mtsho yin/ /las kyis 'khor ba'i sems can rnams/ /chags pa khrag gi rgya mtshor bying / /chags las rnam grol 'gog pa ste/ /chags pa de nyid khrag ces bya/ /khrag gi rgya mtsho bskam pa'i phyir/ /bud med khrag gi rgya mtsho rnams/ /'tsho ba bdud rtsi'i rgya mtshor bsgyur/ /de ltar shes par gyur pa dang / /kun rdzob tshul du 'di ltar sbyar/ /las kyi brtsams pa phun sum tshogs/ /rim pa bzhin du brtsams nas kyang / /maN+Dal 'dom gang gru bzhi la/ /'khor lo bzhi yi thig tu gdab/ /mu khyud phyi rim gru chad bzhi/ /de nas sgo khyams dmar por bya/ /kun gyi phyi rim lag chu hwa'i/ /me ri 'bar bas gtib thag gcad/ /dbus su shar lta zla gam bri/ /ban+d+ha dpal ldan yab yum dgod/ /'khor lo bzhi la rigs bzhir ldan/ /bar khyams gnyis la gnas yul rnams/ /zla gam thig ler ldan par bya/ /sgo khyams sgo bzhi zla gam bcas/ /phyi khyams lag chu hwa yi me/ /me yi khro bo thig ler bcas/ /dur khrod rgyan gyis kun brgyan bya/ /ting 'dzin rdzogs dang dngos bsgrub dang / /'jug pa dbang bskur dngos grub rnams/ /gnas bsrung la sogs rdzogs par bya/ /zhes gsungs so/ /rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po rdo rje bkod pa kun 'dus rig pa'i mdo las 'khor lo dbang sgyur gyi sgrub lugs kyi le'u ste nyi shu rtsa gsum pa'o// //de nas sems dpa'i rdo rje dam pa des 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ /'dus pa chen po'i tshogs chos thams cad ni bdud rtsi sman gyi rang bzhin du shes par bya'o/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar snang ba'i chos thams cad kyi don rtogs na ni 'tsho ba chos nyid kyi rtsi yin/ ma rtogs nas ni 'chi ba 'khor ba'i dug yin/ de bas na chos 'di dag thams cad bdud rtsi'i rang bzhin du shes par bya'o/ /de ltar shes nas kun rdzob tu 'di ltar bsgrub par bya'o/ /ji bzhin 'byung ldan bde sbyar nas/ /
103.93a
ma trang khog pa'i snying ga ru/ /'dom gang tshad dang 'thun pa la/ /rtsibs brgyad 'bar ba'i 'khor lor gdab/ /me yi 'od kyis bskor bar bya/ /rdo rje ra bas bskor ba yi/ /mtha' ma sgo khyud 'bar bar bya/ /dbus su rin chen zur brgyad bya/ /der ni phyag rgya 'bar ba dgod/ /lang ka bsgral ba'i gnas mchog 'dir/ /ral pa can gyi tshogs 'dus te/ /rAk+Sha 'joms pa'i mthu chen kun/ /srid pa gsum ril 'dir sgrol ba'o/ /dus bzhi mchod pa'i dam rdzas kyis/ /de dag ji ltar rigs par mchod/ /dus bzhi bcud smin snying po yis/ /dngos grub chen po'i rdzas su bya/ /phyogs bzhi dbus kyi rdzas chen rnams/ /rmad du byung ba'i ral pa can/ /'byung ba lnga la dbang sgyur mdzad/ /'byung ba lnga yi cho 'phrul sgrub/ /dbyar chu ston me dgun sa ste/ /dbyid rlung nam mkha' gsang bar sbyar/ /cho 'phrul de la dbang thob nas/ /de dag ral pa can du bsgrub/ /ting 'dzin rnam pa lnga gsal bas/ /'byung lnga las byung sha rigs lnga/ /khyi sha ba lang rta sha dang / /bya dang ri dgas sna tshogs ni/ /rdzu 'phrul shugs su sgrub pa'i rdzas/ /sgrub pa'i rdzas chen 'byung chen lnga/ /'jig rten kun la dbang sgyur ba'i/ /de ltar rdzas rnams 'byor pa dang / /ting 'dzin bsgom dang bsgrub pa dang / /thams cad gong dang 'thun sbyar nas/ /'jug dang dngos grub dbang chen rnams/ /ci rigs par ni bde bar sbyar zhes gsungs so/ /bdud rtsi rang byung dkyil 'khor zhes bya ba'i mdo bshad pa'o/ /de nas yang sems dpa'i rdo rje des 'di skad ces gsungs so/ /'dus pa chen po'i rnal 'byor pa/ /gzhan yang bdud rtsi chen po ni/ /gong ma bzhin du legs sbyar nas/ /maN Dal tshad dang 'thun pa la/ /pad ma dmar po 'od kyi mkha'/ /phyi rim zla gam dmar po bzhi/ /rdo rje 'bar bas mdzes par bskor/ /me lce 'bar ba'i phreng ba ni/ /zla gam mtha' zad bri bar bya/ /rin chen ge sar phreng bas ni/ /pad ma'i lce la bskor bar bya/ /sgo bzhi rin chen 'bar bas bya/ /phyag rgya 'bar ba'i lha bkod na/ /
103.93b
dbus su gser phor sul med la/ /dung chen 'khor ba can gyis sbyar/ /shar du shel phor sul 'greng la/ /rin chen mdzod spu gsal bar sbyar/ /lho ru rin chen sul mangs la/ /rin chen lo 'dab rgyas pas sbyar/ /nub tu rgya phor zla gam la/ /bzhin mtshams rin chen 'bur gnyis sbyar/ /byang du bse phor rgya gram la/ /gtsug tor rin chen 'bur bzhi rgyas/ /rtsa ba lnga ni phyogs phyogs sbyar/ /sgo lnga'i gtso bo rigs su sbyar/ /dbus nas shar lho nub byang du/ /ka ko la dang du ru ka /dza ti pha la kha dri zhim/ /lce pog dkar zhes rim par sbyar/ /de bzhin gong gi rim pa bzhin/ /a ru ra dang ga phur dang / /gur kum pad+ma li ga tur/ /de na rA sa yA na rnams/ /thams cad rigs dang kha dog dang / /las dang 'thun par sbyar bar bya/ /sa bon lnga ni rim par sbyar/ /dpal dang ldan pa'i snod nang du/ /yab yum snying po rim bzhin bya/ /dbus dang pad ma lce la dgod/ /gnas yul la sogs mdzes par gzhag /dur khrod rdzas dang bkra shis rdzas/ /'byor pa'i yo byad thams cad bsham/ /de nas byin phab dngos grub gsol/ /thams cad rnam par sbyar bar bya/ /dam pa de nyid gsang chen gyi/ /rigs brgya rigs lnga rigs gcig gis/ /thams cad sbyang ba'i mchog tu bya/ /de nas khrol bu sbyang ba na/ /bsal bsngo bsdu dang dbye ba dang / /khrus bya ba dang bshags pa dang / /yon tan brjod dang byin dbab bya/ /de nas skad cig thang cig gam/ /zhag gcig dag gis sbyar bar bya/ /rtags dag byung na der 'byongs pa'o/ /phye ma'i mchog tu sbyar ba ni/ /snod kyi sman rnams shes rab mas/ /bsdus te btag pa'i cho ga yang / /yum gyis bzung zhing yab kyis btag /rig 'dzin rtsal can dbab cing drang / /so so las kyi sngags brjod cing / /gtan gtun thabs dang shes rab ste/ /sman nyid byang chub sems su sbyar/ /rdo rje glu 'di lha mos blang / /kun tu bzang mo'i gzhal yas su/ /thabs dang shes rab ldan pa las/ /'khor ba bdud rtsi sman du sbyar/ /ye shes lnga ru gsal pa las/ /'bras bu sku gsung thugs su rdzogs/ /
103.94a
'chi med bdud rtsis gcong rnying sbyang / /mtshan ma brtag phyir gcal nas ni/ /rdo rje dpal ldan kha sbyor blugs/ kha dog rigs lnga'i ras kyis bkri/ /rdo rje dbang gi rgya yis gdab/ /rdo rje sngags kyi gzungs kyis gdags/ /dpal chen sku lngar mnga' gsol te/ /ye shes lnga yi dbang bskur bya/ /maN+Dal dag tu dgod par bya/ /kun gyis bskor zhing dngos grub dbab/ /rtsi dang sman gyi bdag po dang / /rtags ldan rig 'dzin phra mo dag /rol mo cha byad mang pos bsten/ /bsgrub pa 'bru mchog gtams pas dgang / /bkra shis gos kyis rgyas par klub/ /gzungs thag gnyer can rigs su dbul/ /ting 'dzin me yis rnam par sbyang / /rtags chen lnga ni gang byung yang / /myur te dngos grub blang bar bya'o/ /bdud rtsi sgra las drangs nas ni/ /dpal ldan pad+ma ldan pa ru/ /thams cad bdud rtsir sa ma ya/ /mkha' klong yangs par bde chen rdzogs/ /rang nyid bdud rtsi'i dkyil 'khor rdzogs/ /gzhan nas bsgrub pa ci yang med/ /'jug pa la sogs thams cad kyang / /tshul bzhin du ni rgyas par bya zhes gsungs so/ /bdud rtsi phye ma'i bsgrub pa rnam par bshad pa'o// //de nas yang sems dpa'i rdo rje des 'di skad ces gsungs so/ /'dus pa chen po'i rnal 'byor pa/ /thams cad de 'drar sbyar nas kyang / /maN+Dal 'khor lo rtsibs brgyad pa/ /phyag rgya'i lha rnams rdzogs byas nas/ /sman sbyang btags btsags gcal nas kyang / /sbrang chang 'o mas gong bur bya/ /bse phor mtshan ldan nang du gzhag /legs par kha sbyar ras kyis dkri/ /gong ma bzhin du kun sbyar nas/ /dngos grub mchog rnams bdag gis bya zhes gsungs so/ /bdud rtsi ri lu'i cho ga rnam par bshad pa'o/ /de nas yang sems dpa'i rdo rje des 'di skad ces gsungs so/ /'dus pa chen po'i rnal 'byor pa/ /skyo ma'i cho ga 'di lta ste/ /thams cad gong ma bzhin sbyar nas/ /mtshan ma gsal po 'byung ba dang / /
103.94b

103.95a

103.95b
mdo las/ bdud rtsi sman gyi bsgrub pa'i le'u ste/ nyi shu rtsa bzhi pa'o// // de nas sems dpa'i rdo rje chen po des bsgrub pa thams cad kyi snying po gsang chen thugs kyi bsgrub pa zhes bya ba 'di bshad do/ /'dus pa chen po'i rnal 'byor pa thams cad ni dbyings su shes par bya ste/ 'khor ba'i chos thams cad ni dbyings su 'dus la/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i chos thams cad ni ye shes su 'dus so/ /de gnyis su med pa ni chos nyid byang chub sems kyi bde ba chen por 'dus par shes par gyis shig /de bas na chos thams cad ni thugs ye shes kyi rang bzhin du 'dus te gnyis su med do/ /de ltar na kun rdzob tu 'di ltar rig par bya ste gnyis su med pa'i don la 'jug par bya'o/ /'dus pa chen po'i rnal 'byor pa/ /dam pa'i don gyi chos rnams kun/ /thams cad rang gi sems la rdzogs/ /kun rdzob chos rnams gang yin pa/ /lus dang ngag la rdzogs par bshad/ /des na chos 'di thams cad kyang / /rtsa ba rang la rdzogs pa ste/ /'di dag bsgrub pa'i thabs mchog kyang / /rnam par rtog pa'i rdul bsal nas/ /bsgrub pa'i rgyal po yab yum gnyis/ /don la mkhas par byas nas ni/ /so so'i thugs la thig le dag /zla gam dkar dmar gdab par bya/ /de yi rdzas mchog chen po yang / /thabs kyi ga pur chen po dang / /shes rab gsang ba'i tsan+dan gnyis/ /dkar dmar zla gam chen por bya/ /yab kyi thugs kar dkar po la/ /thig le kha ni mar lta ba'o/ /yum gyi thugs kar dmar po la/ /thig le kha ni yar lta ba'o/ /yab kyi thig le'i dbus su ni/ /dpal be'u dbus su nyi ma bri/ /dbus su o~M gsal nang du hU~M/ /yum gyi thig le'i dbus su ni/ /pad+ma dbus su zla ba bri/ /dbus su a gsal nang du hU~M/ /de ltar gsal bar gyur pa na/ /kun tu bzang po yab yum du/ /gnyis su med par bsgyur bar bya/ /ting 'dzin gsal bar gyur pa dang / /rang las byung ba'i bdud rtsi yis/ /gsang ba gnyis kyi mchod pa bya/ /rang las byung ba'i dngos
103.96a
grub dag /rang nyid sa ni bstim par bya/ /'di ltar sgrub pa gtsor byed na/ /bdud rtsi'i yo byad thams cad dang / /bcud kyi mchog tu gyur pa rnams/ /lo yi 'tsho bar sbyar nas kyang / /bsnyen sgrub yan lag rnam bzhi las/ /bsnyen pa dag gi dus su ni/ /gang zag mi yi zas la brten/ /de yang lo yi skad cig gam/ /gnyis dang gsum gyi bar du sbyar/ /lo yi skad cig bar du ni/ /bdud rtsi yod byad rnams la brten/ /de nas lo yi skad cig ni/ /gcig gam gnyis kyi bar dag tu/ /rang las byung ba'i rdzas rnam lngas/ /'phags pa mchod cing rang gis bza'/ /des ni drod la gnas par 'gyur/ /drod thob gyur pa phan chad ni/ /lo yi skad cig thang cig gis/ /ting 'dzin zas kyi ro rnyed nas/ kham gyi zas dang bral bar 'gyur/ /drod chen rnam gsum rdzogs nas ni/ /rtags chen dag ni thob par 'gyur/ /rtags kyi cho 'phrul 'byung ba ni/ /rin chen phung po 'dod pa na/ /sa rdo la sogs byas na 'grub/ /chu dang mkha' la 'gro 'dod na/ /brtsams pas mi 'bying thogs med 'gro/ /me yi phung po 'jil 'dod na/ /sdigs pa'i mdzub mo phyar nas kyang / /bden pa'i bsgo ba byas pas 'grub/ /de la sogs pa thams cad nus/ /rtags thob phan chad sangs rgyas yin zhes gsungs so/ /gsang chen thugs kyi bsgrub pa bshad pa'o/ /rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po rdo rje bkod pa kun 'dus rig pa'i rgyud las bka' gsang 'khor lo'i bsgrub pa'i le'u ste/ nyi shu rtsa lnga pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das sems dpa'i rdo rje de rdo rje me glong 'bar ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ /de nas 'dus pa'i tshogs thams cad kyis chos thams cad me'i rang bzhin du snang bar mthong ngo / /de nas 'khor rnams kyis shin tu bstod pa/ /e ma'o sems dpa' che ba che/ /ting 'dzin chen po snang ba che/ /cho 'phrul chen po sna tshogs che/ /thabs mchog khyod la phyag 'tshal lo/ /chos kun me klong bzhin du snang / /
103.96b

103.97a

103.97b

103.101b
yig 'bru 'bar ba'i ga'ur gsal/ /pad+ma 'bar ba'i ga'u 'di/ /yi ge phreng ba 'khyil ba'i gnas/ /dper na me tog 'bar ba las/ /bcud len bung bas bcud blangs te/ /rtsi yi bur bu sog pa ltar/ /dpal be'u thugs kyi dkyil 'khor nas/ /rin chen 'od kyi me tog 'bar/ /ru lu'i yig 'bru bcud kyis rgyas/ /rnal 'byor sems las byas pa yi/ /bcud 'byin bung ba mang po 'phro/ /phar ldings yi ge'i bcud phyung nas/ /tshur ldings sems kyi ga 'ur bstim/ /dang po shel gyi kha dog la/ /shin du gsal zhing 'tsher 'bar ba/ /gnas dgu dag tu zla ba yi/ /thig le dkyil kyi dpal be'u la/ /'bru bkog gsal bar gyur pa dang / /shel gyi bung ba mang po dag /khyung chen ldings ba'i bong tshod tsam/ /phar ldings bcud phyung tshur gsibs pas/ /yig 'bru ye shes me 'bar bas/ /bag chags bud shing phung po bsregs/ /phar spros thugs rjes sa la bskul/ /ji ltar nyi gzer tsha tsha ltar/ /rgyun mi 'chad par rtse gcig 'bar/ /bar du byi ru'i kha dog la/ /gong ma bzhin du bkod gsal la/ /byi ru bung ba mang po dang / /gong ma bzhin du 'phur ldings pas/ /bcud phyung bstim zhing slar la 'phro/ /ji ltar me mgal 'khor tshul du/ /dpal be'u smug po'i klong du bstim/ /kun gyi tha mar bsdu ba ni/ /bkod pa'i gong ma thams cad kun/ /'thing nag 'bar ba bsgyur nas ni/ /khyung chen gzan la 'jums tshod tsam/ /hU~M sgra 'byin cing phan tshun ldings/ /ru lu bcud 'byin dngos grub rlob/ /dran pa'i dkyil nas dza phyung ste/ /lcags kyu 'bar ba ga 'ur btsas/ /dpal be'u 'i dkyil na spungs pa yis/ /ru lu rin chen phung po dag /bsdus shing drangs te gnas su bstim/ /'bab pa'i shugs sam byin brlabs ni/ /mtsho la ser chen 'dril ltar ro/ /'di ltar yi ger sbyar ba'i tshe/ /rnal 'byor nyag gcig ma yin gyi/ /lha mchog dbyings nas bzhugs pa yang / /chos nyid dang du mi dmigs kyang / /rnal 'byor mchog gis bskul ba'i tshe/ /thugs rje chags pa'i mdangs phyung nas/ /srog rtsol dran rig gsung gsung ltar/ /
103.102a

103.102b

103.103a

103.103b

103.105b
rig 'dzin rdo rje rtsal gyi dbang / /rdo rje ming ni sbyin par bya/ /bsgrub pa'i dbang dang rdzas mchog dang / gsang ba'i bdag po yin pas na/ /gsang ba'i dbang mchog sbyin par bya/ /dga' ba byang chub sems chen po/ /kun du tshim par byed pa yi/ /dkar dmar lhag pa'i byang chub sems/ /dbang thob de yi lce la gzhag /btsal med byang chub sems chen po/ /shes rab chen po'i rtsal gyis ni/ /chos sku sgyu mar dbang bsgyur nas/ /rtsal chen rdzogs pa'i dbang yin pas/ /rdzas dang tshig dang gang zag dang / /kun rdzob dbang de ma thob kyang / /chos la sems kyi dbang thob na/ /rgyal ba'i rig 'dzin thams cad dang / /srid gsum dbang can thams cad kun/ /de la dbang thob bskur bar 'gyur/ /dbang gi tshad ni 'di lta ste/ /dad ldan srid zhur ldan pa la/ /gsang ba nyan pa'i dbang chen bskur/ /rnam bzhi las kyi don tshang na/ /las rnams byed pa'i dbang thob bo/ /lta ba'i dmigs bus chos mthong na/ /rgyal theb 'chad pa'i dbang thob bo/ /rkyen thub tshad ma gsum ldan na/ /bla ma rdo rje slob dpon dbang / /dam pa mdzod gsum thams cad la/ /phyogs med par ni 'chad shes nas/ /rab 'byam rgyal po'i dbang 'thob bo/ /dad med blo zhan rdzob pa che/ /tshul 'chos mkhan la ras gcod byed/ /de ni dbang gis 'tshig par bshad/ /gsang med brjed ngas dbang mi 'chags/ /dad med g.yel rmugs dbang mi 'gos/ /snod med bcud bral kun stongs pa/ /des ni dbang thob ma yin no/ /snod ldan bcud rdzogs dbang thob na/ /dbang mchog thob pa'i rgyu zhes bshad/ /ces gsungs so// //
103.106a
rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po rdo rje bkod pa kun 'dus rig pa'i mdo las rdo rje dbang gi le'u zhes bya ste sum cu rtsa gnyis pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po dang / sems dpa'i rdo rje dam pa rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po kun 'dus rig pa'i mdo dang bcas pa chos thams cad kyi me long yin par rig nas/ 'dus pa phal mo che'i 'khor rnams kyis shin du ngam zhing ngo mtshar skyes nas/ bstod pa shin tu dga' ba chen po'i glu 'di blangs so/ /e ma hoH nyes bcom legs ldan mtshan zhi mtha' las 'das/ /dpag med byams snyoms don gyis bdag gzhan dpal/ /don dam gsang sbas nam mkha'i dkyil du 'khyil/ /rdo rje che mchog dbang phyug kun gyi bdag /'dzin pa mi rtog sha rus khrag la rol/ /thugs kyi gdung thag 'khor ba'i mtha' la rje/ /yul med ma skyes mtshan ma'i g.yul las rgyal/ /bde mchog rgyal po khyod la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /shes rab chen po nam mkha'i nyi mar gsal/ /byang chub sems kyi 'od zer dbyings su 'char/ /dpa' brtul myur ba'i shugs kyis 'gro drug sgrol/ /rtog 'joms ye shes rdo rje cho 'phrul 'phro/ /dam pa'i don gsungs gnyis med ston pa'i sku/ /smra ba'i seng ge khyod la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rin chen gter ldan 'dod dgur kun skong zhing / /lung dang rigs pa gtan tshigs kun gyi mdzod/ /brda can yang dag len pa'i me long gsal/ /rdo rje kun 'dus 'jigs byed rgyal ba'i rgyud/ /chos kyi me long 'di la bdag cag 'dud/ /rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po rdo rje bkod pa kun 'dus rig pa'i mdo las ngo mtshar bstod pa'i le'u ste sum bcu rtsa gsum pa'o// //rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po rdo rje bkod pa kun 'dus rig pa'i mdo rdzogs so// // bkra shis so/ dge'o/ /
